# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
App Overview ^CKKx6aDu

users ^AA9V01BL

admins ^5BHxAaix

Managers ^8TKfpoYX

Users/Techs ^xLyIWbAx

Individual Obsidian vaults; Setup prompt to install Obsidian + install 'Local REST API' Community plugin.
Individual vaults sync with Master Vault through tiered + adjustable review process ^nuca80cp

Can assign users/techs documents to revise/create as well as create groups of users/techs to peer edit/create certain documentation or categories of documentation together.
Determines final approval of documentation before sending it to the 'Master Team Vault', which is also synced via the 'Git Vault' Community plugin allowing the vault to be stored as a 
private GitHub repo. This will also be present in the master library section of the dashboard, which allows users of all tiers to read and check out all of the finalized documentation.  ^7AACIF6C

Manages the Master Vault Repo, organization, roles, etc. ^2p3NwBx2
